FROM [ContentPage] AS [c]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c0].[Id], [c0].[BannerButtonText], [c0].[BannerText], [c0].[ButtonLink], [c0].[ButtonText], [c0].[ContentData], [c0].[ContentOrderNo], [c0].[ContentPageId], [c0].[ContentShort], [c0].[ContentTypesId], [c0].[CreaDate], [c0].[CreaUser], [c0].[Description], [c0].[EndDate], [c0].[ExternalLink], [c0].[FormTypeId], [c0].[IsActive], [c0].[IsClick], [c0].[IsDeleted], [c0].[IsFooterMenu], [c0].[IsGallery], [c0].[IsHamburgerMenu], [c0].[IsHeaderMenu], [c0].[IsHome], [c0].[IsMap], [c0].[IsPublish], [c0].[IsSideMenu], [c0].[IsStatus], [c0].[LangId], [c0].[Link], [c0].[LoginCount], [c0].[MetaDescription], [c0].[MetaKeywords], [c0].[MetaTitle], [c0].[ModDate], [c0].[ModUser], [c0].[Name], [c0].[OrderNo], [c0].[OrjId], [c0].[OrjId1], [c0].[StartDate], [c0].[TemplateType], [c0].[VideoLink]
    FROM [ContentPage] AS [c0]
    WHERE [c0].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t] ON [c].[ContentPageId] = [t].[Id]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d].[Id], [d].[Alt], [d].[BannerImageId], [d].[CreaDate], [d].[CreaUser], [d].[DocumentId], [d].[GalleryId], [d].[Guid], [d].[IsDeleted], [d].[IsStatus], [d].[Link], [d].[LoginCount], [d].[ModDate], [d].[ModUser], [d].[Name], [d].[OrderNo], [d].[PictureId], [d].[ThumbImageId], [d].[Title], [d].[Types], [d].[data_class]
    FROM [Documents] AS [d]
    WHERE [d].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t0] ON [c].[Id] = [t0].[ThumbImageId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d0].[Id], [d0].[Alt], [d0].[BannerImageId], [d0].[CreaDate], [d0].[CreaUser], [d0].[DocumentId], [d0].[GalleryId], [d0].[Guid], [d0].[IsDeleted], [d0].[IsStatus], [d0].[Link], [d0].[LoginCount], [d0].[ModDate], [d0].[ModUser], [d0].[Name], [d0].[OrderNo], [d0].[PictureId], [d0].[ThumbImageId], [d0].[Title], [d0].[Types], [d0].[data_class]
    FROM [Documents] AS [d0]
    WHERE [d0].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t1] ON [c].[Id] = [t1].[PictureId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d1].[Id], [d1].[Alt], [d1].[BannerImageId], [d1].[CreaDate], [d1].[CreaUser], [d1].[DocumentId], [d1].[GalleryId], [d1].[Guid], [d1].[IsDeleted], [d1].[IsStatus], [d1].[Link], [d1].[LoginCount], [d1].[ModDate], [d1].[ModUser], [d1].[Name], [d1].[OrderNo], [d1].[PictureId], [d1].[ThumbImageId], [d1].[Title], [d1].[Types], [d1].[data_class]
    FROM [Documents] AS [d1]
    WHERE [d1].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t2] ON [c].[Id] = [t2].[BannerImageId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c1].[Id], [c1].[BannerButtonText], [c1].[BannerText], [c1].[ButtonLink], [c1].[ButtonText], [c1].[ContentData], [c1].[ContentOrderNo], [c1].[ContentPageId], [c1].[ContentShort], [c1].[ContentTypesId], [c1].[CreaDate], [c1].[CreaUser], [c1].[Description], [c1].[EndDate], [c1].[ExternalLink], [c1].[FormTypeId], [c1].[IsActive], [c1].[IsClick], [c1].[IsDeleted], [c1].[IsFooterMenu], [c1].[IsGallery], [c1].[IsHamburgerMenu], [c1].[IsHeaderMenu], [c1].[IsHome], [c1].[IsMap], [c1].[IsPublish], [c1].[IsSideMenu], [c1].[IsStatus], [c1].[LangId], [c1].[Link], [c1].[LoginCount], [c1].[MetaDescription], [c1].[MetaKeywords], [c1].[MetaTitle], [c1].[ModDate], [c1].[ModUser], [c1].[Name], [c1].[OrderNo], [c1].[OrjId], [c1].[OrjId1], [c1].[StartDate], [c1].[TemplateType], [c1].[VideoLink]
    FROM [ContentPage] AS [c1]
    WHERE [c1].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t3] ON [c].[Id] = [t3].[ContentPageId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d2].[Id], [d2].[Alt], [d2].[BannerImageId], [d2].[CreaDate], [d2].[CreaUser], [d2].[DocumentId], [d2].[GalleryId], [d2].[Guid], [d2].[IsDeleted], [d2].[IsStatus], [d2].[Link], [d2].[LoginCount], [d2].[ModDate], [d2].[ModUser], [d2].[Name], [d2].[OrderNo], [d2].[PictureId], [d2].[ThumbImageId], [d2].[Title], [d2].[Types], [d2].[data_class]
    FROM [Documents] AS [d2]
    WHERE [d2].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t4] ON [c].[Id] = [t4].[GalleryId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d3].[Id], [d3].[Alt], [d3].[BannerImageId], [d3].[CreaDate], [d3].[CreaUser], [d3].[DocumentId], [d3].[GalleryId], [d3].[Guid], [d3].[IsDeleted], [d3].[IsStatus], [d3].[Link], [d3].[LoginCount], [d3].[ModDate], [d3].[ModUser], [d3].[Name], [d3].[OrderNo], [d3].[PictureId], [d3].[ThumbImageId], [d3].[Title], [d3].[Types], [d3].[data_class]
    FROM [Documents] AS [d3]
    WHERE [d3].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t5] ON [c].[Id] = [t5].[DocumentId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [s].[Id], [s].[ContentPageId], [s].[ContentValue], [s].[CreaDate], [s].[CreaUser], [s].[IsDeleted], [s].[IsStatus], [s].[LangId], [s].[LoginCount], [s].[ModDate], [s].[ModUser], [s].[OrderNo], [s].[SpecId]
    FROM [SpecContentValue] AS [s]
    WHERE [s].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t6] ON [c].[Id] = [t6].[ContentPageId]
WHERE [c].[IsDeleted] IS NULL AND (([c].[IsPublish] = CAST(1 AS bit)) AND ([c].[IsActive] = CAST(1 AS bit)))
ORDER BY [c].[Id], [t].[Id], [t0].[Id], [t1].[Id], [t2].[Id], [t3].[Id], [t4].[Id], [t5].[Id], [t6].[Id]"

    FROM [Documents] AS [d1]
    WHERE [d1].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t2] ON [c].[Id] = [t2].[BannerImageId]

    FROM [ContentPage] AS [c1]
    WHERE [c1].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t3] ON [c].[Id] = [t3].[ContentPageId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d2].[Id], [d2].[Alt], [d2].[BannerImageId], [d2].[CreaDate], [d2].[CreaUser], [d2].[DocumentId], [d2].[GalleryId], [d2].[Guid], [d2].[IsDeleted], [d2].[IsStatus], [d2].[Link], [d2].[LoginCount], [d2].[ModDate], [d2].[ModUser], [d2].[Name], [d2].[OrderNo], [d2].[PictureId], [d2].[ThumbImageId], [d2].[Title], [d2].[Types], [d2].[data_class]
    FROM [Documents] AS [d2]
    WHERE [d2].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t4] ON [c].[Id] = [t4].[GalleryId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d3].[Id], [d3].[Alt], [d3].[BannerImageId], [d3].[CreaDate], [d3].[CreaUser], [d3].[DocumentId], [d3].[GalleryId], [d3].[Guid], [d3].[IsDeleted], [d3].[IsStatus], [d3].[Link], [d3].[LoginCount], [d3].[ModDate], [d3].[ModUser], [d3].[Name], [d3].[OrderNo], [d3].[PictureId], [d3].[ThumbImageId], [d3].[Title], [d3].[Types], [d3].[data_class]
    FROM [Documents] AS [d3]
    WHERE [d3].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t5] ON [c].[Id] = [t5].[DocumentId]
WHERE [c].[IsDeleted] IS NULL AND (([c].[IsPublish] = CAST(1 AS bit)) AND ([c].[IsActive] = CAST(1 AS bit)))
ORDER BY [c].[Id], [t].[Id], [t0].[Id], [t1].[Id], [t2].[Id], [t3].[Id], [t4].[Id], [t5].[Id]"
